I understand the burnout thing. I started my current channel (which is just song covers) a few years ago for fun, but it's been hard to maintain, with my day job hours being all over the place and liable to change at any time, and also COVID ruining most of my motivation to do anything for most of 2020 (also I work at a grocery store so once lockdowns started I started having to work a lot more hours suddenly). I've also been focusing more on my writing, which is what I actually WANT to do as a career. It's been hard to balance all that stuff, and I think I too have been becoming a workhorse as a result. So I will probably need to take a break soon. I need to recharge, watch TV shows I'm behind on, play video games I want to play (case in point: I got Nintendo Switch Sports not long after it came out in April, and it's July and I still haven't played it), etc. Or if I do write, do something easier. I did that for Camp NaNo April this year. Since I just finished a novel manuscript in March, I just wrote a fanfic for Camp, and was surprised to see how easily things flowed. So once I finish my current project I'll probably do something similar for at least a month. Not just to relax, but like you I also need to make some branding decisions, since I'm transitioning into more of a promotion stage as an author, and I failed miserably at building a platform last time I tried ~2009 cause I had no clue what I was doing.  Anyways hope you enjoy your sabbatical, and in the meantime I'll probably watch your old Let's Plays and such. I'm watching the B2W2 Metronome Randomizer Nuzlocke series right now. Aside from the amusement of following PM7's absurd bad luck streak, it's made me want to go back and finish the Gen 5 games cause I never finished them (to be fair when they came out I was in like my last year-ish of college, and also working part-time, so I was very busy). Tho TBH I've been focusing on my 3DS more than my Switch recently anyway since the eShop is shutting down soon.  Also the Galarian Runerigus thing reminded me of how they label regional evolutions (like Runerigus) like they are regional forms in the TCG, even though they are not regional forms of previous PokÃ©mon, like the Hisuian starters or Alolan Raichu, but actual new PokÃ©mon. The arc phone sounds like "park" or "dark" where it's a *hard c.* Arceus is pronounced either ARKOOS if you're an MandJTV fan or for most pokemon fans, are-see-us. The reason for this is because of the rule where the letter c becore e, i, or y is an s sound, like in the words sit or hiss. Example words would be celery for c before e, cinder for c before i, and cyan for c before y.  So to conclude, Arc phone is pronounced  /É‘rk foÊŠn/, and Arceus is pronounced /aarÂ·seeÂ·uhs/
